`WithTracingHTTPLoggingAttributes()` function (line 14): Extracts trace context from request headers\\n   - `spanContextFromHeaders()` function (line 37): Uses `otel.GetTextMapPropagator().Extract()` (line 40) for header-based extraction\\n\\n6. **pkg/apiserver/endpoints/filters/jaeger_tracing.go** (WithExtractJaegerTrace, line 11): Jaeger-specific trace context extraction:\\n   - Uses `propagation.TraceContext{}` to extract from custom `Grafana-Upstream-Traceparent` header (line 20)\\n\\n## Prometheus/Prometheus\\n\\nPrometheus implements OpenTelemetry trace context propagation for scraping and remote read/write operations:\\n\\n1. **tracing/tracing.go**: Main tracing manager:\\n   - HTTP client transport is wrapped with `otelhttp.NewTransport()` for automatic trace context injection during scrape operations (line 2265)\\n\\n## Trace Context Propagation Pattern Summary\\n\\nAll three projects implement OpenTelemetry trace context propagation using:\\n- **Injection**: Using `otel.GetTextMapPropagator().Inject()` or `tracer.Inject()` to add trace context to HTTP headers and gRPC metadata\\n- **Extraction**: Using `otel.GetTextMapPropagator().Extract()` to read trace context from incoming request headers\\n- **Propagators**: W3C TraceContext (standard) and optionally Jaeger propagators for cross-service trace correlation\\n- **Automatic Propagation**: Via `otelhttp.NewHandler()` and `otelhttp.NewTransport()` which automatically handle extraction from incoming requests and injection into outgoing requests\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
